GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*exp(-Abs(x))*v - mu*(c1 - v**c2)*v
Candidate formulas: 54

GT (fixed) simplifies to a concrete function of \((x,t,v)\):
\[
F(x,t,v)=0.3852302349\sin t\;-\;0.1114436972\,v\,e^{-|x|}\;-\;0.3325884184\,v\;+\;0.3325884184\,v^3\;-\;0.05896131021\,v^3
\]
So the polynomial-in-\(v\) part is
- linear term: \(-0.3325884184\,v\)
- cubic term: \((0.3325884184-0.05896131021)\,v^3 = 0.2736271082\,v^3\)

Thus GT has exactly these structural components:
1) a pure \(\sin(t)\) term (no \(x,v\) inside),
2) a linear-in-\(v\) term,
3) a cubic-in-\(v\) term,
4) a term \(v\exp(-|x|)\) **with absolute value** in the exponent,
and **no** constants, no \(x\)-only terms, no \(t\)-polynomials/logs, no \(v\)-logs, etc.

Key obstruction: candidates generally have \(v\exp(c\,x)\) (no \(|x|\)). Because \(x\) can be negative, there is no real constant \(c\) such that \(\exp(c x)\equiv \exp(-|x|)\) for all real \(x\). (For \(x\ge 0\), \(\exp(-|x|)=\exp(-x)\); for \(x<0\), \(\exp(-|x|)=\exp(x)\). A single \(c\) cannot satisfy both.)

Now check each candidate.

1. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3+c4 e^{c5 t}+c6 v+c7 v^3+c8 v e^{c9 x}\)  
   Can match \(\sin t\) via phase/frequency (set \(c1=1,c2=0\), \(c0=0.385...\)). Set \(c3=0\), \(c4=0\). Match linear/cubic via \(c6,c7\). But \(v e^{c9 x}\) cannot equal \(v e^{-|x|}\) globally. **No.**

2. Same issue as (1) with \(t^{c4}\) term removable by \(c3=0\), but still \(e^{c9 x}\) vs \(e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

3. Has \(c0 x\) (must set \(c0=0\)), has \(v e^{c6 x}\) (same absolute-value problem), extra \(v\sin(\cdot)\) must be zeroed. Still cannot create \(e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

4. \(c0 v^3 + c1\cos(c2+t)+ c3 v e^{c4 x}+ c5 v\sin(\cdot)\).  
   Cos can become sin by phase shift: \(\cos(t+\phi)=\sin(t+\phi+\pi/2)\), so OK. Set \(c5=0\). Still \(e^{c4 x}\neq e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

5. Includes \(c3 t\) (set \(c3=0\)), otherwise same as (1) with \(e^{c8 x}\) issue. **No.**

6. Has \(c0 x\) (set 0), \(v e^{c6 x}\) issue, plus \(v(c8+t)^{c9}\) must be 0. **No.**

7. Same: \(v e^{c4 x}\) cannot match \(v e^{-|x|}\); extra \(v(c6+t)^{c7}\) must be 0. **No.**
